BAPTIST HEALTH®
BAPTIST HEALTH MEDICAL GROUP
PATIENT CONDITIONS AND CONSENTS
1. CONSENT TO DIAGNOSTIC TESTS, PROCEDURES, & MEDICAL TREATMENT:
| voluntarily consent to care involving routine diagnostic tests, procedures and medical treatment as ordered by my treating physician(s), including
their assistants or designees. In the case of diagnostic studies, | consent to the interpretation of the studies at an off-site location through the use of
telehealth. | consent to medical, nursing, allied health and other students observing and participating in my care under the supervision of a qualified
professional. | consent to photographic recordings or reproducible images during the surgical, medical, and/or diagnostic procedure(s) and their
use for scientific, educational, identification, or research purposes. | also consent to testing for communicable and blood-borne infectious diseases,
such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV), if a provider orders testing for diagnostic purposes or if there has
been an exposure to healthcare personnel. | have been given no guarantees about the results that may be obtained from my care.
2. PHYSICIANS AND OTHER HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS WHO ARE NOT EMPLOYEES OF BAPTIST HEALTH MEDICAL GROUP:
In most situations, the medical treatment provided to patients by Baptist Health Medical Group (“Baptist”) is provided by Baptist employed physicians
and providers. However, there other providers who are not employees or agents of Baptist that may provide medical services or be involved in my
care. Such providers include, but are not limited to radiologists, pathologists, and psychologists. These providers may be independent or may be
employed by other health care organizations. You may receive a separate bill for the services of these providers or the bill you receive may have
separate charges for services of such providers. Charges for such services are established by these providers.
3. CONSENT TO USE AND DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION:
| authorize Baptist to use and disclose information about me to carry out treatment, payment and healthcare operations. Examples of such uses and
disclosures include, but are not limited to, providing information to: (a) any person, company, or entity (such as HMOs, insurance companies,
workers’ compensation carriers, my employer, the Medicare and Medicaid programs and their intermediaries and review organizations, and any
other payor or its review organization or third party administrator) that is or may be liable for paying any claim for benefits arising out of services
provided to me by Baptist; (b) any health care provider or ambulance company providing services for me; (c) any providers who may be providing
ongoing care to me such as hospitals, home health agencies, nursing homes, physicians, and other health care facilities; (d) any licensing or
accrediting organizations necessary for Baptist to obtain or maintain licensure or accreditation; (e) to providers or entities for the purposes of
conducting medical audits, utilization reviews, or quality assurance reviews; and (f) any other persons or entities described in Baptist’s Notice of
Privacy Practices. This consent includes the release of medical records and billing information related to drug-related conditions, alcoholism,
psychological and psychiatric conditions, and/or communicable or blood-borne infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human
immunodeficiency virus (HIV). | also consent to any third party payor or its review organization paying for my care to discuss my plan of treatment for
utilization review purposes. | also authorize the release of my social security number to the manufacturer of any implanted medical device in
accordance with the Medical Device Tracking Act.
4. FINANCIAL AGREEMENT AND ASSIGNMENT OF BENEFITS:
| agree that | am responsible for payment of my physician office bill. Payment of any portion of my bill not covered by a third party payor is due at the
time of service unless Baptist has agreed to other arrangements.
| agree to the assignment of all third party payor benefits to Baptist and to any health care provider rendering services to me. | agree to pay Baptist
and other health care providers for all charges for services that are not covered or paid by any third party payor regardless of the reason, including but
not limited to a determination by any third party payor that such services are not covered services or medically necessary. To the extent | ama
Medicare or Medicaid beneficiary, |certify that any information | provide in applying for payment under Title XVIII (Medicare) or Title XIX (Medicaid) of the
Social Security Act is correct. | request payment of authorized benefits to be made on my behalf to Baptist or to any health care provider rendering
services to me by the Medicare or Medicaid program. | hereby irrevocably appoint Baptist as my authorized representative to pursue any claims,
penalties, and administrative and/or legal remedies on my behalf for collection against any responsible payer, employer-sponsored medical benefit
plans, third party liability carrier or, any other responsible third party for any and all benefits due me for the payment of charges associated with my
treatment. This assignment shall not be construed as an obligation of Baptist to pursue any such right of recovery. | agree to take all actions
necessary to assist Baptist in collecting payment from any such third party payer.
After reasonable notice, any unpaid account may be turned over to a collection agency and/or attorney for collection. Should it be necessary for
Baptist to pursue collection, | agree to pay all reasonable collection costs, including court costs and attorney’s fees incurred by Baptist in collecting
my account.
Pursuant to the Fair Credit Reporting Act (15 USC §1681b(a)(2)), | authorize SearchAmerica, or any other a credit reporting agency, to release to

5. SMOKE-FREE ENVIRONMENT:
Baptist maintains a smoke-free environment at each of its locations. Smoking is prohibited by health care personnel, patients, and visitors.

Baptist programs and activities are available regardless of race, color, national origin, religion, sex, disability or any other status protected by federal,
state or local law.

10. CONSENT TO WIRELESS TELEPHONE CALLS:
| hereby authorize Baptist and all third parties, including clinical providers who have provided care to me, along with any billing services, collection
agencies, attorneys or other agents who may work on their behalf (including their successors, assigns, affiliates, or agents), to contact me at any
telephone number associated with my account(s), including wireless telephone numbers or other numbers that may result in charges to me. |
agree that methods of contact may include using automatic telephone dialing systems or other computer assisted technology.
11. CONSENT TO EMAILOR TEXT USAGE FOR HEALTHCARE COMMUNICATIONS:
If at any time | provide an email address at which | may be contacted, | consent to receiving healthcare communication at that email from Baptist. |
further consent to Baptist communicating healthcare information, such as appointment reminders, to me on my wireless telephone through text.

authorizes Baptist or its designee to represent patient during any appeal process. The undersigned certifies that he/she has read and agrees to this

prescriptions are picked up.
Please note written prescriptions will not be given to anyone youhave not listed as an authorized pick up. If at any
time you wouldlike tomake changes toyour approved list, youmay do so bycompleting a new authorization form.

[DOB-206] - Clinical Documentation Only in BAPTIST HEALTH CORBIN SOUTH IMAGING MRI (continued) · Call 911 or have someone take you to the Emergency Department if you have any of the following: · Sudden numbness or weakness of your face, arm or leg especially on one side of the body
· Sudden confusion, difficulty speaking or trouble understanding
· Changes in your vision or loss of sight in one eye
· Sudden severe headache with no known cause
· Sudden dizziness, trouble walking, loss of balance or coordination
It is important to seek emergency care right away if you have further stroke symptoms. If you get
emergency help quickly, the powerful clot-dissolving medicines can reduce the disabilities caused by a
stroke. 
For more information:
American Stroke Association
1-888-4-STROKE
www.strokeassociation.org
IF YOU SMOKE OR USE TOBACCO PLEASE READ THE FOLLOWING:
Why is smoking bad for me?
Smoking increases the risk of heart disease, lung disease, vascular disease, stroke, and cancer. If you
smoke, STOP!
For more information:
Quit Now Kentucky
1-800-QUIT-NOW
https://kentucky.quitlogix.org/en-US/
If you feel like life is too tough and are thinking of suicide or injuring yourself, get help right away! · Call or text 988 to speak to someone.

Narrative:
MRI HUMERUS LEFT WO CONTRAST- REASON FOR EXAM: M25.512; M54.2-Cervicalgia; M25.512-Pain in left
shoulder
COMPARISON: Plain films of the humerus dated [DOB-279]
Scans were obtained through the left humerus in the sagittal, axial and
coronal planes using T1 and T2-weighted scans. MRI Findings: In the mid shaft of the humerus there is some increased
signal focally in the cortical bone of the humerus. This increased
signal is on both the T1 and T2 scans. The marrow signal was
unremarkable. There is no edema in the area of the periosteum. Muscles
in the arm were unremarkable. No other areas of abnormal signal are
noted in the humerus.
Impression:
Focal abnormal signal in the cortical bone of the mid shaft
of humerus on both the T1 and T2 sequences. This could represent
hemangioma. Would recommend consideration of bone scan especially in the
setting of pain in this region for further evaluation. This report was finalized on 5/27/2022 8:06 AM by Dr. William Daniel II, MD.

INPATIENT AND OUTPATIENT CONDITIONS AND CONSENTS CSN: 91131427492 ADMIT DATE:
1. CONSENT TO DIAGNOSTIC TESTS, PROCEDURES, & MEDICALTREATMENT:| voluntarily consent to (and consent on behalf of any
child born to me while hospitalized) care involving routine diagnostic tests, procedures and medical treatment as ordered by my
admitting and treating physicians, including their assistants or designees. | consent to receive medical care through the use of
telehealth and/or remote patient monitoring. |further consent to the interpretation of diagnostic studies from an off-site location using
telehealth technologies. | consent to medical, nursing, allied health and other students observing and participating in my care under the
supervision of a qualified professional. | consent to photographic recordings or reproducible images during the surgical, medical, and/or
diagnostic procedure(s) and their use for identification, scientific, educational, or research purposes. |also consent to testing for
communicable and blood-borne infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV), if a
provider orders testing for diagnostic purposes or if there has been an exposure to healthcare personnel. | have been given no
guarantees about the results that may be obtained from my care. | understand and agree that the results of diagnostic tests, procedures
and medical treatment ordered and provided by providers while | am hospitalized, including a notice of admission to the hospital, a
notice of discharge from the hospital, and/or notice of transfer from the hospital to another facility will be provided to my primary care
physician, physician group and/or post acute care provider on record, if any.
2. PHYSICIANS AND OTHER HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS WHO ARE NOT EMPLOYEES OF THE HOSPITAL: Physicians and certified
registered nurse anesthetists rendering medical treatment to patients in the hospital are not employed by the Hospital. In most
situations, advanced practitioners, including but not limited to, nurse practitioners, physician assistants, surgical assistants and
psychologists, providing treatment to patients inthe Hospital are not employed by the Hospital. You may receive a separate bill for the
services of these providers, or the Hospital bill you receive may have separate charges for services of such providers. Charges for such
services are established by the providers.
3. FINANCIAL AGREEMENT AND ASSIGNMENT OF BENEFITS:| agree that | am responsible for payment of my Hospital bill. Payment
of any portion of my bill not covered by a third party payor is due upon discharge from the Hospital unless the Hospital has agreed to
other arrangements. | agree to the assignment of all third party payor benefits to the Hospital and to any health care provider rendering
services to me. | acknowledge and agree that Hospital is not required to accept assignment of any third party payor benefits, in which
case, | may receive a bill from Hospital for the full amount of charges related to any care or treatment provided to me or my guarantee by
Hospital and | agree to pay the Hospital and other health care providers for such charges. Moreover, |understand that Hospital may
accept payment from third party payors with whom itdoes not have a written signed agreement and that such acceptance of payment
does not constitute acceptance by Hospital of any reimbursement rates established by such third party payors and that | may receive a
bill from Hospital for the difference between the rate paid by such third party payors and the Hospital’s charges. | agree to pay the
Hospital and other health care providers for all charges for services that are not covered or paid by any third party payor regardless of the
reason, including but not limited to a determination by any third party payor that such services are not covered services or medically
necessary. To the extent |am a Medicare or Medicaid beneficiary, | certify that any information | provide inapplying for payment under
Title XVIII (Medicare) or Title XIX (Medicaid) of the Social Security Act is correct. | request payment of authorized benefits to be made on
my behalf to Baptist Health facility or to any health care provider rendering services to me by the Medicare or Medicaid program. |
hereby irrevocably appoint Hospital as my authorized representative to pursue any claims, penalties, and administrative and/or legal
remedies on my behalf for collection against any responsible payer, employer-sponsored medical benefit plans, third party liability
carrier or, any other responsible third party for any and all benefits due me for the payment of charges associated with my treatment.
This assignment shall not be construed as an obligation of the Hospital to pursue any such right of recovery. | agree to take all actions
necessary to assist Hospital in collecting payment from any such third party payer. | understand that after reasonable notice, any
unpaid account may be turned over to a collection agency and/or attorney for collection. Should it be necessary for the Hospital to
pursue collection, | agree to pay all reasonable collection costs, including court costs and attorney’s fees incurred by the Hospital in
collecting my account. Pursuant to the Fair Credit Reporting Act (15 USC §1681b(a)(2)), | authorize a credit reporting agency engaged
by Hospital or its collection agents to release to the Hospital or any of its representatives or affiliates, my consumer report. |
understand that the purpose of this authorization and request is to obtain my consumer report, which may be used to determine the
availability of or the need for financial assistance, charity care, or insurance coverage for me and may be used for billing and collection
purposes related to payment for services provided to me. | understand this authorization is valid until my Hospital account for all
services is closed.

Notice of Hospital Based Services
| understand that the services | am receiving today are being provided by Baptist Health and
will be billed by Baptist Health.
| understand that my out of pocket responsibility for deductibles, coinsurance, copayments and
so forth may be higher than if | received these services at a physician office, a freestanding
center or a reference laboratory. | understand that what | am paying today reflects an estimated
deposit only and that | will be billed for the remaining balance.
| understand that the exact amount |owe will be determined by my insurance coverage based
on the terms of my benefit plan. | understand that the claim for the services | receive will be
coded based on coding guidelines for a hospital outpatient facility. | understand that Baptist
Health is unable to change the coding on a claim to reduce out of pocket responsibility.
Because this is a Baptist Health hospital outpatient location, you may receive multiple billing
statements reflecting both hospital and professional charges associated with your visit(s).
| also understand that other providers, such as radiologists, may bill for the professional
component of services | receive today and will bill separately for those services.

INPATIENT AND OUTPATIENT CONDITIONS AND CONSENTS CSN: 91066360989 ADMIT DATE:
1. CONSENT TO DIAGNOSTIC TESTS, PROCEDURES, & MEDICALTREATMENT:| voluntarily consent to (and consent on behalf of any child born to
me while hospitalized) care involving routine diagnostic tests, procedures and medical treatment as ordered by my admitting and treating
physicians, including their assistants or designees. In the case of diagnostic studies, | consent to the interpretation of the studies at an off-site
location through the use of telehealth. | consent to medical, nursing, allied health and other students observing and participating in my care
under the supervision of a qualified professional. | consent to photographic recordings or reproducible images during the surgical, medical,
and/or diagnostic procedure(s) and their use for identification, scientific, educational, or research purposes. | also consent to testing for
communicable and blood-borne infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV), if a provider
orders testing for diagnostic purposes or if there has been an exposure to healthcare personnel. | have been given no guarantees about the
results that may be obtained from my care.
2. PHYSICIANS AND OTHER HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS WHO ARE NOT EMPLOYEES OF THE HOSPITAL: Physicians and certified registered
nurse anesthetists rendering medical treatment to patients in the hospital are not employed by the Hospital. In most situations, advanced
practitioners, including but not limited to, nurse practitioners, physician assistants, surgical assistants and psychologists, providing
treatment to patients in the Hospital are not employed by the Hospital. You may receive a separate bill for the services of these providers, or
the Hospital bill you receive may have separate charges for services of such providers. Charges for such services are established by the
providers.
3. CONSENT TO USE AND DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION: |authorize the Hospital and the health care providers on its medical staff to use
and disclose information about me to carry out treatment, payment and healthcare operations. Examples of such uses and disclosures
include, but are not limited to, providing information to: (a) any person, company, or entity (Such as HMOs, insurance companies, workers’
compensation carriers, my employer, the Medicare and Medicaid programs and their intermediaries and review organizations, and any
other payor or its review organization or third party administrator) that is or may be liable for paying any claim for benefits arising out of
services provided to me on an inpatient or outpatient basis, or for any ambulance services provided for my transport to or from the Hospital;
(b) any health care provider or ambulance company providing services for me; (c) any providers who may be providing follow-up care to me
after discharge such as home health agencies, nursing homes, physicians, and other health care facilities to which the patient may be
transferred; (d) any licensing or accrediting organizations necessary for the Hospital to obtain or maintain licensure or accreditation; (e) to
providers or entities for the purposes of conducting medical audits, utilization reviews, or quality assurance reviews; and (f) any other
persons or entities described in the Hospital’s Notice of Privacy Practices. This consent includes the release of medical records and billing
information related to drug-related conditions, alcoholism, psychological and psychiatric conditions, and/or communicable or blood-borne
infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV). | also consent to any third party payor or
its review organization paying for my care to discuss my plan of treatment for utilization review purposes. | also authorize the release of my
social security number to the manufacturer of any implanted medical device in accordance with the Medical Device Tracking Act.
4. FINANCIAL AGREEMENT ANDASSIGNMENT OF BENEFITS:| agree that | am responsible for payment of my Hospital bill. Payment of any
portion of my bill not covered by a third party payor is due upon discharge from the Hospital unless the Hospital has agreed to other
arrangements. | agree to the assignment of all third party payor benefits to the Hospital and to any health care provider rendering services to
me. | agree to pay the Hospital and other health care providers for all charges for services that are not covered or paid by any third party
payor regardless of the reason, including but not limited to a determination by any third party payor that such services are not covered
services or medically necessary. To the extent | am a Medicare or Medicaid beneficiary, | certify that any information | provide in applying for
payment under Title XVIII (Medicare) or Title XIX (Medicaid) of the Social Security Act is correct. | request payment of authorized benefits to be
made on my behalf to Baptist Health facility or to any health care provider rendering services to me by the Medicare or Medicaid program. |
hereby irrevocably appoint Hospital as my authorized representative to pursue any claims, penalties, and administrative and/or legal
remedies on my behalf for collection against any responsible payer, employer-sponsored medical benefit plans, third party liability carrier or,
any other responsible third party for any and all benefits due me for the payment of charges associated with my treatment. This assignment
shall not be construed as an obligation of the Hospital to pursue any such right of recovery. | agree to take all actions necessary to assist
Hospital in collecting payment from any such third party payer. | understand that after reasonable notice, any unpaid account may be turned
over to a collection agency and/or attorney for collection. Should it be necessary for the Hospital to pursue collection, | agree to pay all
reasonable collection costs, including

5. OUTPATIENT MEDICARE PATIENTS: Medicare does not cover prescription drugs with only a few exceptions. According to Medicare
regulations, | acknowledge that | am responsible for any drugs furnished to me while an outpatient that meet Medicare’s definition of a
prescription drug. These drugs are also referred to as self-administered but they may be administered to me by Hospital personnel.
Medicare requires Hospital to bill Medicare patients or other third party payers for these drugs. Medicare Part D beneficiaries may submit a
paper claim to the Medicare Part D Plan for possible reimbursement of these drugs in accordance with Medicare Drug Plan enrollment
materials.
6. HOSPITAL IS NOT RESPONSIBLE FOR LOSS OF PERSONAL ARTICLES: | UNDERSTAND THAT THE HOSPITAL MAINTAINS A SAFE FOR
THE SAFEKEEPING OF MONEY ANDVALUABLESAND THAT THE HOSPITAL IS NOT LIABLE FOR THE LOSS OF OR DAMAGE TO MONEY,
JEWELRY, GLASSES, DENTURES, DOCUMENTS, CLOTHING, OR OTHER ITEMS OF PERSONAL PROPERTY.
7. SMOKE-FREE ENVIRONMENT: This Hospital maintains a smoke-free environment on its campus. Smoking is prohibited by health care
personnel, patients, and visitors on the Hospital’s campus. | understand that | am to remain in my treatment area at all times. | further
understand that if | leave my treatment area, | will not be under nursing or medical supervision, and further understand that leaving my
treatment area may complicate or interfere with the course of treatment prescribed by my physician.
8. NOTICE OF NONDISCRIMINATION: Hospital programs and activities are available regardless of race, color, national origin, religion, sex
(including gender identity and gender stereotyping), disability or any other status protected by federal, state or local law.

PREVENTING SURGICAL SITE INFECTIONS
· Call 911 or have someone take you to the Emergency Department if you have any of the following: · Sudden numbness or weakness of your face, arm or leg especially on one side of the body
· Sudden confusion, difficulty speaking or trouble understanding
· Changes in your vision or loss of sight in one eye
· Sudden severe headache with no known cause
· Sudden dizziness, trouble walking, loss of balance or coordination
It is important to seek emergency care right away if you have further stroke symptoms. If you get
emergency help quickly, the powerful clot-dissolving medicines can reduce the disabilities caused by a
stroke. 
For more information:
American Stroke Association
1-888-4-STROKE
www.strokeassociation.org

FINDINGS:
Vertebral body height and alignment are intact. Modic type changes are present at the C3/4 level. Marrow signal
otherwise unremarkable throughout. Cervical spinal cord demonstrates no mass, edema, or syrinx. The posterior elements are intact. The prevertebral soft tissues are within normal limits. Cervical medullary junction and visualized portions of posterior fossa
are unremarkable. C2/3: Unremarkable. C3/4: Disc osteophyte complex and small central posterior disc
protrusion. Moderate central canal stenosis. Effacement of the ventral
thecal sac. There is mild right-sided neural foraminal stenosis. C4/5: Unremarkable. C5/6: Unremarkable. C6/7: Unremarkable. C7/T1: Unremarkable.
Impression:
1. Degenerative disc disease and small superimposed disc protrusion at
C3/4 causing moderate central canal and mild right-sided neural
foraminal stenosis. 2. Otherwise unremarkable exam. This report was finalized on 6/22/2019 11:50 AM by Dr. Kevin J Croce, MD.

Health is unable to change the coding on a claim to reduce out of pocket responsibility.

INPATIENT AND OUTPATIENT CONDITIONS AND CONSENTS CSN: 91063233676 ADMIT DATE:
1. CONSENT TO DIAGNOSTIC TESTS, PROCEDURES, & MEDICALTREATMENT:| voluntarily consent to (and consent on behalf of any child born to
me while hospitalized) care involving routine diagnostic tests, procedures and medical treatment as ordered by my admitting and treating
physicians, including their assistants or designees. In the case of diagnostic studies, | consent to the interpretation of the studies at an off-site
location through the use of telehealth. | consent to medical, nursing, allied health and other students observing and participating in my care
under the supervision of a qualified professional. | consent to photographic recordings or reproducible images during the surgical, medical,
and/or diagnostic procedure(s) and their use for identification, scientific, educational, or research purposes. | also consent to testing for
communicable and blood-borne infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV), if a provider
orders testing for diagnostic purposes or if there has been an exposure to healthcare personnel. | have been given no guarantees about the
results that may be obtained from my care.
2. PHYSICIANS AND OTHER HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS WHO ARE NOT EMPLOYEES OF THE HOSPITAL: Physicians and certified registered
nurse anesthetists rendering medical treatment to patients in the hospital are not employed by the Hospital. In most situations, advanced
practitioners, including but not limited to, nurse practitioners, physician assistants, surgical assistants and psychologists, providing
treatment to patients in the Hospital are not employed by the Hospital. You may receive a separate bill for the services of these providers, or
the Hospital bill you receive may have separate charges for services of such providers. Charges for such services are established by the
providers.
3. CONSENT TO USE AND DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION: |authorize the Hospital and the health care providers on its medical staff to use
and disclose information about me to carry out treatment, payment and healthcare operations. Examples of such uses and disclosures
include, but are not limited to, providing information to: (a) any person, company, or entity (Such as HMOs, insurance companies, workers’
compensation carriers, my employer, the Medicare and Medicaid programs and their intermediaries and review organizations, and any
other payor or its review organization or third party administrator) that is or may be liable for paying any claim for benefits arising out of
services provided to me on an inpatient or outpatient basis, or for any ambulance services provided for my transport to or from the Hospital;
(b) any health care provider or ambulance company providing services for me; (c) any providers who may be providing follow-up care to me
after discharge such as home health agencies, nursing homes, physicians, and other health care facilities to which the patient may be
transferred; (d) any licensing or accrediting organizations necessary for the Hospital to obtain or maintain licensure or accreditation; (e) to
providers or entities for the purposes of conducting medical audits, utilization reviews, or quality assurance reviews; and (f) any other
persons or entities described in the Hospital’s Notice of Privacy Practices. This consent includes the release of medical records and billing
information related to drug-related conditions, alcoholism, psychological and psychiatric conditions, and/or communicable or blood-borne
infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV). | also consent to any third party payor or
its review organization paying for my care to discuss my plan of treatment for utilization review purposes. | also authorize the release of my
social security number to the manufacturer of any implanted medical device in accordance with the Medical Device Tracking Act.
4. FINANCIAL AGREEMENT ANDASSIGNMENT OF BENEFITS:| agree that | am responsible for payment of my Hospital bill. Payment of any
portion of my bill not covered by a third party payor is due upon discharge from the Hospital unless the Hospital has agreed to other
arrangements. | agree to the assignment of all third party payor benefits to the Hospital and to any health care provider rendering services to
me. | agree to pay the Hospital and other health care providers for all charges for services that are not covered or paid by any third party
payor regardless of the reason, including but not limited to a determination by any third party payor that such services are not covered
services or medically necessary. To the extent | am a Medicare or Medicaid beneficiary, | certify that any information | provide in applying for
payment under Title XVIII (Medicare) or Title XIX (Medicaid) of the Social Security Act is correct. | request payment of authorized benefits to be
made on my behalf to Baptist Health facility or to any health care provider rendering services to me by the Medicare or Medicaid program. |
hereby irrevocably appoint Hospital as my authorized representative to pursue any claims, penalties, and administrative and/or legal
remedies on my behalf for collection against any responsible payer, employer-sponsored medical benefit plans, third party liability carrier or,
any other responsible third party for any and all benefits due me for the payment of charges associated with my treatment. This assignment
shall not be construed as an obligation of the Hospital to pursue any such right of recovery. | agree to take all actions necessary to assist
Hospital in collecting payment from any such third party payer. | understand that after reasonable notice, any unpaid account may be turned
over to a collection agency and/or attorney for collection. Should it be necessary for the Hospital to pursue collection, | agree to pay all
reasonable collection costs, including

5. OUTPATIENT MEDICARE PATIENTS: Medicare does not cover prescription drugs with only a few exceptions. According to Medicare
regulations, | acknowledge that | am responsible for any drugs furnished to me while an outpatient that meet Medicare’s definition of a
prescription drug. These drugs are also referred to as self-administered but they may be administered to me by Hospital personnel.
Medicare requires Hospital to bill Medicare patients or other third party payers for these drugs. Medicare Part D beneficiaries may submit a
paper claim to the Medicare Part D Plan for possible reimbursement of these drugs in accordance with Medicare Drug Plan enrollment
materials.
6. HOSPITAL IS NOT RESPONSIBLE FOR LOSS OF PERSONAL ARTICLES: | UNDERSTAND THAT THE HOSPITAL MAINTAINS A SAFE FOR
THE SAFEKEEPING OF MONEY ANDVALUABLESAND THAT THE HOSPITAL IS NOT LIABLE FOR THE LOSS OF OR DAMAGE TO MONEY,
JEWELRY, GLASSES, DENTURES, DOCUMENTS, CLOTHING, OR OTHER ITEMS OF PERSONAL PROPERTY.
7. SMOKE-FREE ENVIRONMENT: This Hospital maintains a smoke-free environment on its campus. Smoking is prohibited by health care
personnel, patients, and visitors on the Hospital’s campus. | understand that | am to remain in my treatment area at all times. | further
understand that if | leave my treatment area, | will not be under nursing or medical supervision, and further understand that leaving my
treatment area may complicate or interfere with the course of treatment prescribed by my physician.
8. NOTICE OF NONDISCRIMINATION: Hospital programs and activities are available regardless of race, color, national origin, religion, sex
(including gender identity and gender stereotyping), disability or any other status protected by federal, state or local law.

PREVENTING SURGICAL SITE INFECTIONS
· Call 911 or have someone take you to the Emergency Department if you have any of the following: · Sudden numbness or weakness of your face, arm or leg especially on one side of the body
· Sudden confusion, difficulty speaking or trouble understanding
· Changes in your vision or loss of sight in one eye
· Sudden severe headache with no known cause
· Sudden dizziness, trouble walking, loss of balance or coordination
It is important to seek emergency care right away if you have further stroke symptoms. If you get
emergency help quickly, the powerful clot-dissolving medicines can reduce the disabilities caused by a
stroke. 
For more information:
American Stroke Association
1-888-4-STROKE
www.strokeassociation.org

Why is smoking bad for me?
Smoking increases the risk of heart disease, lung disease, vascular disease, stroke, and cancer. If you
smoke, STOP!

INPATIENT AND OUTPATIENT CONDITIONS AND CONSENTS CSN: 91061122470 ADMIT DATE:
1. CONSENT TO DIAGNOSTIC TESTS, PROCEDURES, & MEDICALTREATMENT:| voluntarily consent to (and consent on behalf of any child born to
me while hospitalized) care involving routine diagnostic tests, procedures and medical treatment as ordered by my admitting and treating
physicians, including their assistants or designees. In the case of diagnostic studies, | consent to the interpretation of the studies at an off-site
location through the use of telehealth. | consent to medical, nursing, allied health and other students observing and participating in my care
under the supervision of a qualified professional. | consent to photographic recordings or reproducible images during the surgical, medical,
and/or diagnostic procedure(s) and their use for identification, scientific, educational, or research purposes. | also consent to testing for
communicable and blood-borne infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV), if a provider
orders testing for diagnostic purposes or if there has been an exposure to healthcare personnel. | have been given no guarantees about the
results that may be obtained from my care.
2. PHYSICIANS AND OTHER HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS WHO ARE NOT EMPLOYEES OF THE HOSPITAL: Physicians and certified registered
nurse anesthetists rendering medical treatment to patients in the hospital are not employed by the Hospital. In most situations, advanced
practitioners, including but not limited to, nurse practitioners, physician assistants, surgical assistants and psychologists, providing
treatment to patients in the Hospital are not employed by the Hospital. You may receive a separate bill for the services of these providers, or
the Hospital bill you receive may have separate charges for services of such providers. Charges for such services are established by the
providers.
3. CONSENT TO USE AND DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION: |authorize the Hospital and the health care providers on its medical staff to use
and disclose information about me to carry out treatment, payment and healthcare operations. Examples of such uses and disclosures
include, but are not limited to, providing information to: (a) any person, company, or entity (Such as HMOs, insurance companies, workers’
compensation carriers, my employer, the Medicare and Medicaid programs and their intermediaries and review organizations, and any
other payor or its review organization or third party administrator) that is or may be liable for paying any claim for benefits arising out of
services provided to me on an inpatient or outpatient basis, or for any ambulance services provided for my transport to or from the Hospital;
(b) any health care provider or ambulance company providing services for me; (c) any providers who may be providing follow-up care to me
after discharge such as home health agencies, nursing homes, physicians, and other health care facilities to which the patient may be
transferred; (d) any licensing or accrediting organizations necessary for the Hospital to obtain or maintain licensure or accreditation; (e) to
providers or entities for the purposes of conducting medical audits, utilization reviews, or quality assurance reviews; and (f) any other
persons or entities described in the Hospital’s Notice of Privacy Practices. This consent includes the release of medical records and billing
information related to drug-related conditions, alcoholism, psychological and psychiatric conditions, and/or communicable or blood-borne
infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV). | also consent to any third party payor or
its review organization paying for my care to discuss my plan of treatment for utilization review purposes. | also authorize the release of my
social security number to the manufacturer of any implanted medical device in accordance with the Medical Device Tracking Act.
4. FINANCIAL AGREEMENT ANDASSIGNMENT OF BENEFITS:| agree that | am responsible for payment of my Hospital bill. Payment of any
portion of my bill not covered by a third party payor is due upon discharge from the Hospital unless the Hospital has agreed to other
arrangements. | agree to the assignment of all third party payor benefits to the Hospital and to any health care provider rendering services to
me. | agree to pay the Hospital and other health care providers for all charges for services that are not covered or paid by any third party
payor regardless of the reason, including but not limited to a determination by any third party payor that such services are not covered
services or medically necessary. To the extent | am a Medicare or Medicaid beneficiary, | certify that any information | provide in applying for
payment under Title XVIII (Medicare) or Title XIX (Medicaid) of the Social Security Act is correct. | request payment of authorized benefits to be
made on my behalf to Baptist Health facility or to any health care provider rendering services to me by the Medicare or Medicaid program. |
hereby irrevocably appoint Hospital as my authorized representative to pursue any claims, penalties, and administrative and/or legal
remedies on my behalf for collection against any responsible payer, employer-sponsored medical benefit plans, third party liability carrier or,
any other responsible third party for any and all benefits due me for the payment of charges associated with my treatment. This assignment
shall not be construed as an obligation of the Hospital to pursue any such right of recovery. | agree to take all actions necessary to assist
Hospital in collecting payment from any such third party payer. | understand that after reasonable notice, any unpaid account may be turned
over to a collection agency and/or attorney for collection. Should it be necessary for the Hospital to pursue collection, | agree to pay all
reasonable collection costs, including

Medicare requires Hospital to bill Medicare patients or other third party payers for these drugs. Medicare Part D beneficiaries may submit a
paper claim to the Medicare Part D Plan for possible reimbursement of these drugs in accordance with Medicare Drug Plan enrollment
materials.

· G44.89 (ICD-10-CM) - Headache syndrome
PREVENTING SURGICAL SITE INFECTIONS
· Call 911 or have someone take you to the Emergency Department if you have any of the following: · Sudden numbness or weakness of your face, arm or leg especially on one side of the body
· Sudden confusion, difficulty speaking or trouble understanding
· Changes in your vision or loss of sight in one eye
· Sudden severe headache with no known cause
· Sudden dizziness, trouble walking, loss of balance or coordination

no evidence of acute ischemia

1. CONSENT TO DIAGNOSTIC TESTS, PROCEDURES, & MEDICALTREATMENT:| voluntarily consent to (and consent on behalf of any child born to
me while hospitalized) care involving routine diagnostic tests, procedures and medical treatment as ordered by my admitting and treating
physicians, including their assistants or designees. In the case of diagnostic studies, | consent to the interpretation of the studies at an off-site
location through the use of telehealth. | consent to medical, nursing, allied health and other students observing and participating in my care
under the supervision of a qualified professional. | consent to photographic recordings or reproducible images during the surgical, medical,
and/or diagnostic procedure(s) and their use for identification, scientific, educational, or research purposes. | also consent to testing for
communicable and blood-borne infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV), if a provider
orders testing for diagnostic purposes or if there has been an exposure to healthcare personnel. | have been given no guarantees about the
results that may be obtained from my care.
2. PHYSICIANS AND OTHER HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS WHO ARE NOT EMPLOYEES OF THE HOSPITAL: Physicians and certified registered
nurse anesthetists rendering medical treatment to patients in the hospital are not employed by the Hospital. In most situations, advanced
practitioners, including but not limited to, nurse practitioners, physician assistants, surgical assistants and psychologists, providing
treatment to patients in the Hospital are not employed by the Hospital. You may receive a separate bill for the services of these providers, or
the Hospital bill you receive may have separate charges for services of such providers. Charges for such services are established by the
providers.
3. CONSENT TO USE AND DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION: |authorize the Hospital and the health care providers on its medical staff to use
and disclose information about me to carry out treatment, payment and healthcare operations. Examples of such uses and disclosures
include, but are not limited to, providing information to: (a) any person, company, or entity (Such as HMOs, insurance companies, workers’
compensation carriers, my employer, the Medicare and Medicaid programs and their intermediaries and review organizations, and any
other payor or its review organization or third party administrator) that is or may be liable for paying any claim for benefits arising out of
services provided to me on an inpatient or outpatient basis, or for any ambulance services provided for my transport to or from the Hospital;
(b) any health care provider or ambulance company providing services for me; (c) any providers who may be providing follow-up care to me
after discharge such as home health agencies, nursing homes, physicians, and other health care facilities to which the patient may be
transferred; (d) any licensing or accrediting organizations necessary for the Hospital to obtain or maintain licensure or accreditation; (e) to
providers or entities for the purposes of conducting medical audits, utilization reviews, or quality assurance reviews; and (f) any other
persons or entities described in the Hospital’s Notice of Privacy Practices. This consent includes the release of medical records and billing
information related to drug-related conditions, alcoholism, psychological and psychiatric conditions, and/or communicable or blood-borne
infectious diseases, such as hepatitis, tuberculosis, and the human immunodeficiency virus (HIV). | also consent to any third party payor or
its review organization paying for my care to discuss my plan of treatment for utilization review purposes. | also authorize the release of my
social security number to the manufacturer of any implanted medical device in accordance with the Medical Device Tracking Act.

me. | agree to pay the Hospital and other health care providers for all charges for services that are not covered or paid by any third party
payor regardless of the reason, including but not limited to a determination by any third party payor that such services are not covered
services or medically necessary. To the extent | am a Medicare or Medicaid beneficiary, | certify that any information | provide in applying for
payment under Title XVIII (Medicare) or Title XIX (Medicaid) of the Social Security Act is correct. | request payment of authorized benefits to be

Patient Instructions
None · Call 911 or have someone take you to the Emergency Department if you have any of the following: · Sudden numbness or weakness of your face, arm or leg especially on one side of the body
· Sudden confusion, difficulty speaking or trouble understanding
· Changes in your vision or loss of sight in one eye
· Sudden severe headache with no known cause
· Sudden dizziness, trouble walking, loss of balance or coordination
It is important to seek emergency care right away if you have further stroke symptoms. If you get
emergency help quickly, the powerful clot-dissolving medicines can reduce the disabilities caused by a
stroke. 
For more information:
American Stroke Association
1-888-4-STROKE
www.strokeassociation.org
IF YOU SMOKE OR USE TOBACCO PLEASE READ THE FOLLOWING:
Why is smoking bad for me?
Smoking increases the risk of heart disease, lung disease, vascular disease, stroke, and cancer. If you
smoke, STOP!
For more information:
Quit Now Kentucky
1-800-QUIT-NOW
https://kentucky.quitlogix.org/en-US/
If you feel like life is too tough and are thinking of suicide or injuring yourself, get help right away! · Call or text 988 to speak to someone. *** END OF REPORT ***
